<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:синеть.html>сине́ть</a> (12861)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синий.html>си́ний</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sínij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синеть.html>сине́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sinétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посинеть.html>посине́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn/become blue</li>
<li><i>(skin)</i> to turn blue/livid
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:синеть.html>сине́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>холода</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sinétʹ</b> ot xoloda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn blue with cold</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to appear/show blue
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдали.html>вдали́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:синеть.html>сине́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ре</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vdalí <b>sinéjet</b> móre</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the sea appears (deep) blue in the distance; the (deep) blue sea is seen in the distance</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***синий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:синий.html>си́ний</a> (721)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*siňь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синий.html>си́ний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sínij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:синий.html>сине́е</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:синий.html>сине́й</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сине́йший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deep blue
<dl><dd></dd></dl></li>
<li>indigo
<dl><dd></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dead <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sense transferred from the blue color of a dead person's face</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> drunken, drunk <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also acts as noun</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> being a thief belonging to the Russian mafia <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from the blue color of the tattoos that cover his body</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синий.html>си́ний</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sínij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голубо́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">golubój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (different shades of blue) are seen as distinct basic colors in Russian, as different from each other as blue and green would be for an English speaker; Russian does not have one single color term corresponding to blue.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Adjectives</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">светло́-си́ний</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svetló-sínij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">тёмно-си́ний</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tjómno-sínij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синеватый.html>синева́тый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sinevátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синенький.html>си́ненький</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sínenʹkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синюшный.html>синю́шный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sinjušnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:синица.html>сини́ца</a> (19319)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sinica</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синица.html>сини́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">siníca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синица.html>сини́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синица.html>сини́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синица.html>сини́ц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>titmouse, tomtit (any bird of the family Paridae)</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, двувидовой (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образовывать.html>образо́вывать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 2a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-синтез-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-ир-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ова</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***синька.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:синька.html>си́нька</a> (27249)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синька.html>си́нька</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sínʹka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синька.html>си́ньки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синька.html>си́ньки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синька.html>си́нек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bluing (blue pigment used for coloring clothes when washing)</li>
<li>blueprint (paper-based reproduction usually of a technical drawing), diazo print, ammonia print</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> drunkenness, drinking
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замерзнуть.html>замёрз</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:синька.html>си́ньке</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zamjórz po <b>sínʹke</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he <b>got drunk</b> and froze to death</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синяк.html>синя́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sinják</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синяк.html>синяка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синяк.html>синяки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:синяк.html>синяко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bruise (medical: mark on the skin)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>Echium</i>, a genus of flowering plant in the family Boraginaceae</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a hard drinking person, drunkard</li></ol>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> orphan; orphan's
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сиротский.html>сиро́тская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sirótskaja</b> žiznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>orphan's</b> life</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> poor, miserable</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> orphan care
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сиротский.html>сиро́тский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sirótskij</b> dom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">orphanage</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>orphan-care</b> house</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
